\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03050}03050 \textcolor{comment}{  /// A class for elements that allow the imposition of a displacement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03051}03051 \textcolor{comment}{  /// constraint for bulk solid elements via a Lagrange multiplier.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03052}03052 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Prescribed displaced is obtained from an adjacent bulk solid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03053}03053 \textcolor{comment}{  /// element (rather than from a lower-\/dimensional GeomObject}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03054}03054 \textcolor{comment}{  /// as in the corresponding ImposeDisplacementByLagrangeMultiplierElement}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03055}03055 \textcolor{comment}{  /// class. The present class is particularly suited for parallel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03056}03056 \textcolor{comment}{  /// FSI computations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03057}03057 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)b NOTE: Currently (and for the foreseeable future) this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03058}03058 \textcolor{comment}{  /// element only works with bulk elements that do not have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03059}03059 \textcolor{comment}{  /// generalised degrees of freedom (so it won't work with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03060}03060 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Hermite-\/type elements, say). The additional functionality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03061}03061 \textcolor{comment}{  /// to deal with such elements could easily be added (once a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03062}03062 \textcolor{comment}{  /// a suitable test case is written). For now we simply throw}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{solid__traction__elements_8h_source_l03063}03063 \textcolor{comment}{  /// errors if an attempt is made to use the element with an unsuitable}}
